local oldHttpGet
oldHttpGet = hookfunction(game.HttpGet, function(self, url, ...)
    print(url)
    local res = oldHttpGet(self, url, ...)
    print(res)
        if url and url:find("/?hwid") and not url:find('_NTTo') then
        warn("[HttpGet] Fake /get-key response")
        return [[
_G.index_key = "KEY_363636"
_G.left = 36363
]]
    end
    return res
end)

-- Version 71
_G.credit = [[Obfucator NTT - https://discord.gg/YAdrT39SWq]]
local function VM1(bytecode)
    local stack = {}
    local sp = 0
    local ip = 1
    while true do 
        local opcode = bytecode[ip]
        ip = ip + 1 
        if opcode == 0 then 
            sp = sp + 1
            stack[sp] = bytecode[ip]
            ip = ip + 1 
        elseif opcode == 1 then 
            local value = stack[sp]
            sp = sp - 1 
            stack[sp] = stack[sp] + value 
        elseif opcode == 2 then 
            local value = stack[sp]
            sp = sp - 1 
            stack[sp] = stack[sp] - value 
        elseif opcode == 3 then 
            local value = stack[sp]
            sp = sp - 1
            stack[sp] = stack[sp] * value
        elseif opcode == 4 then
            local value = stack[sp]
            sp = sp - 1
            stack[sp] = stack[sp] / value
        elseif opcode == 5 then
            return stack[sp] or 0
        else
            return 0
        end
    end
end
